<script id="deposit-launch" type="text/javascript">
        

    $(document).ready(function() {
   
        //find the container
        var _container = $('.deposit-container');
        if( _container.size() == 0 )
        {
            $('<div class="deposit-container"></div>').appendTo($('body'));
            _container = $('.deposit-container');
        }
            
        var inline = _container.hasClass('deposit-inline');
             
        $('.deposit-launch').each( function(){
            	 
            $(this).bind('click', function(event){
                var config = {
                       url: "/eco/teller/deposit.ajax",
                       mode: inline ? '' : 'modal'
                };
                var deposit = new Deposit(_container[0], config);
                deposit.init();
            });	 
        });    
   });

function doLaunchDeposit( )
  {
      var  container = $('.deposit-container');
      if (container.size() == 0) {
             $('<div class="deposit-container"></div>').appendTo($('body'));
             container = $('.deposit-container');
     }
      var config = {
             url: "/eco/teller/deposit.ajax",
             mode: 'modal'
      };
      var deposit = new Deposit(container, config);
      deposit.init();
  }

   </script>

	function iOSversion() {
		if (/iP(hone|od|ad)/.test(navigator.platform)) {
			var v = (navigator.appVersion).match(/OS (\d+)_(\d+)_?(\d+)?/);
			return [parseInt(v[1], 10), parseInt(v[2], 10), parseInt(v[3] || 0, 10)];
		}
	}
	var iOSversion = iOSversion();
	if (iOSversion && iOSversion[0] < 8) {

var getUrl = function() {
    return decodeURIComponent(window.location.pathname);
};

var getRefer = function() {
    return document.referrer;
};

var referRegEx = new RegExp( "(belmont\.ag)" );

    if ( referRegEx.test( getRefer() ) ){

 	function loadMBJ() {
 
 	 var sportType = $.cookie("ruibj");
 	 var mbjGameUrl = getMiniBJURLBySport(sportType )['miniBJUrl'];
 	 $("#bj-url").html('<iframe src="' + mbjGameUrl + '" allowtransparency="true" name="miniframe" id="miniframe" width="100%" height="200" frameborder="0" scrolling="no"  marginheight="0" marginwidth="0"></iframe>');
 
 	}
 
 	function getMiniBJURLBySport() {
 	   var sportType = $.cookie("ruibj");
 		var gameUrl = jsonMiniBJURLMap[sportType];
 		var imageUrl = jsonMiniBJImageMap[sportType];
 		
 		
 		if(typeof gameUrl == 'undefined'){
 			gameUrl = jsonMiniBJURLMap['default'];
 		}
 		
 		if(typeof imageUrl == 'undefined'){
 			imageUrl = jsonMiniBJImageMap['default'];
 		}
 		
 		var urlArray = new Array();
 		urlArray['miniBJUrl'] = gameUrl;
 		urlArray['miniBJImageUrl'] = imageUrl;
 		
 		return urlArray;
 	}	
 		
 
 	$('#bj-img').attr('src', getMiniBJURLBySport()['miniBJImageUrl']);
